综合案例1-爬取西安地区短租房信息¶

1 本节目标¶

利用 requests库、BeautifulSoup库爬取小猪短租网西安地区短租房的信息。

2 爬虫思路分析¶

（1）网站URL分析¶

通过前4页网址寻找URL变化规律

第一页：https://xa.xiaozhu.com

第二页：https://xa.xiaozhu.com/search-duanzufang-p2-0/

第三页：https://xa.xiaozhu.com/search-duanzufang-p3-0/

第四页：https://xa.xiaozhu.com/search-duanzufang-p4-0/

URL的构造：只需更改P后的数字即可。https://xa.xiaozhu.com/search-duanzufang-p2-0/

In [151]:
#以前12页为例：
for i in range(13):
    url='https://xa.xiaozhu.com/search-duanzufang-p'+str(i)+'-0/'
    print(url)

https://xa.xiaozhu.com/search-duanzufang-p0-0/
https://xa.xiaozhu.com/search-duanzufang-p1-0/
https://xa.xiaozhu.com/search-duanzufang-p2-0/
https://xa.xiaozhu.com/search-duanzufang-p3-0/
https://xa.xiaozhu.com/search-duanzufang-p4-0/
https://xa.xiaozhu.com/search-duanzufang-p5-0/
https://xa.xiaozhu.com/search-duanzufang-p6-0/
https://xa.xiaozhu.com/search-duanzufang-p7-0/
https://xa.xiaozhu.com/search-duanzufang-p8-0/
https://xa.xiaozhu.com/search-duanzufang-p9-0/
https://xa.xiaozhu.com/search-duanzufang-p10-0/
https://xa.xiaozhu.com/search-duanzufang-p11-0/
https://xa.xiaozhu.com/search-duanzufang-p12-0/

（2）爬取的内容需要进入详细页网址链接进行爬取¶

（3）需要爬取的信息：标题、地址、价格、房东名称、房东性别、房东头像的链接¶

3 爬虫实战¶

本部分从请求网页开始，一步步进行。

（1）网页请求¶

In [152]:
import requests
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup

以爬一页上的店铺的信息为例：

In [153]:
#1 请求网页并获取网页源码
In [160]:
header={"User-Agent":"Mozilla/5.0 (Macintosh; Intel Mac OS X 10_15_3) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/80.0.3987.116 Safari/537.36"}
In [162]:
response=requests.get("https://xa.xiaozhu.com/",headers=header)
print(response.status_code)

200
In [163]:
re=response.text
print(re)

import json
for i in range(len(url_son)):
    res_son=requests.get(url_son[i],headers=header)
    soup_son=BeautifulSoup(res_son.text,'lxml')
    dict={}
    dict['title']=soup_son.find_all('em')[1].string
    dict['dizhi']=soup_son.find_all(class_="pr5")[0].string
    dict['price']=soup_son.find_all(class_="day_l")[0].text
    
    with open('house.txt','a',encoding='utf-8') as f:
        f.write(json.dumps(dict,ensure_ascii=False)+'\n')

爬取一页代码整理¶

In [213]:
import requests
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup
import json

header={"User-Agent":"Mozilla/5.0 (Macintosh; Intel Mac OS X 10_15_3) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/80.0.3987.116 Safari/537.36"}
response=requests.get("https://xa.xiaozhu.com/",headers=header)
re=response.text

soup=BeautifulSoup(re,'lxml')
soup

url_son=[]
for i in range(len(soup.find_all('div',attrs={'class':'result_btm_con lodgeunitname'}))):
    url_son.append(soup.find_all('div',attrs={'class':'result_btm_con lodgeunitname'})[i].attrs['detailurl'])
for i in range(len(url_son)):
    res_son=requests.get(url_son[i],headers=header)
    soup_son=BeautifulSoup(res_son.text,'lxml')
    dict={}
    dict['title']=soup_son.find_all('em')[1].string
    dict['dizhi']=soup_son.find_all(class_="pr5")[0].string
    dict['price']=soup_son.find_all(class_="day_l")[0].text
    with open('house.txt','a',encoding='utf-8') as f:
        f.write(json.dumps(dict,ensure_ascii=False)+'\n')

爬取多页¶

In [214]:
import requests
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup
import json
import time
header={"User-Agent":"Mozilla/5.0 (Macintosh; Intel Mac OS X 10_15_3) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/80.0.3987.116 Safari/537.36"}
for i in range(13):#点击下一页，翻页
    time.sleep(2)
    url='https://xa.xiaozhu.com/search-duanzufang-p'+str(i)+'-0/'
    response=requests.get(url,headers=header)
    re=response.text
    soup=BeautifulSoup(re,'lxml')
    url_son=[]
    for i in range(len(soup.find_all('div',attrs={'class':'result_btm_con lodgeunitname'}))):#获取每一页商家的页面url
        url_son.append(soup.find_all('div',attrs={'class':'result_btm_con lodgeunitname'})[i].attrs['detailurl'])
    for i in range(len(url_son)):#每一个商家的信息
        res_son=requests.get(url_son[i],headers=header)
        soup_son=BeautifulSoup(res_son.text,'lxml')
        dict={}
        dict['title']=soup_son.find_all('em')[1].string
        dict['dizhi']=soup_son.find_all(class_="pr5")[0].string
        dict['price']=soup_son.find_all(class_="day_l")[0].text
        with open('house.txt','a',encoding='utf-8') as f:
            f.write(json.dumps(dict,ensure_ascii=False)+'\n')
In [ ]:
备注：该网站存在滑块反扒问题，目前没有讲到滑块的问题，如果代码报错，打开网页，手动拉取滑块后，运行程序就可以爬取了。
